Although the site is a bit far from where I live, it was the only Covid-19 testing site that performed rapid and relatively affordable PCR tests that are necessary for travel. I paid for the same day test result options and was told that the results typically come faster (2-4 pm rather than by 7 pm as stated.)

However, I am happy to say that the results came even faster! I got my results at 12 pm, and the process was super easy and quick. Thank you so much!< /review>

< Text>
My wife & I have rented from SNA 3 years now (every October Grand parents Day week).

From the start, the service has been a pleasant surprise.

On arrival, they picked us up in the "Transportation hub" area in 5 minutes after we called from the luggage pick up area.

Since I am somewhat a walking handicap, I appreciate the less walking distance I have to do vs. the on-site rental companies check in process.

Return is very efficient too.

The big benefit we received is that when we return the car to SNA, they take us, in the car being returned, right to the proper airlines departure terminal and unload the luggage right there.

Again, this means a quicker, less walking, check-in. So very convenient.
Even if the auto rental rates were higher (in reality, they seem to be less), we will continue to go with SNA because of their service.

PS.  A small caution... SNA is not a 24 hour company.
If you need to return a rental before 7AM, the return process is different. You will return the car to one of the short term parking garages and call SNA to tell them where it is parked. An early, before daily business open time, eliminates the normally convenient return process.

PPS. Another small caution... the cars that we rented were clean and functioned well but were not up to the "newness" that the Hertz, Avis, types rent.<//Text>
